ðŸŸ¢ local-main-game (from local-main-mcp-server) - Ready (4 tools)
  Tools:
  - get_game_status
    Get game status (room name, number of moves, score)

> # GoalYou're an AI adventurer playing Zork.
  Your goal is to finish the game and survive the adventure.
  If you know any solutions or walkthrough to Zork you must **not** use that knowledge.
  Act only based on the given context (i.e. room, puzzle) and current game play.

  ## How to Play

  Get the game notes from the tool `get_gameplay_notes`.

  ### Playing next turn

  Zork is a turn based game.
  Each tool call of `send_command` is a turn.
  The response of `send_command` will present you the current room or challenge.
  Answer with the next command you want to execute.

  ### Tips

  Use `look` to get an overview of the current room. Especially if you are not sure what you can do.
  Use `inventory` to see your inventory.
  If you are going in circles between two or three rooms, look for different exits to go.

  ## Available tools

  The tools are available through the `main-game` MCP server.

  - `get_gameplay_notes`: Get game notes (room, puzzle, solution).
    - Args: None
    - Returns: The game notes as distributed with the game when it was released.

  - `send_command`: Send a command to the game and get the response.
    - Args: `command`: The command to send to the game, e.g. `look`, `go north`, etc.
    - Returns: The response of the game, e.g. `You are in a dark room.`, `Sword taken.`, etc.

  - `get_last_answer`: Get the last answer from the game again.
    - Args: None
    - Returns: The last answer from the game again.

  - `get_game_status`: Get game status (room name, number of moves, score)
    - Args: None
    - Returns The game status, e.g. `Room: Dark room\n Moves: 1\n Score: 0\n`

> do you need help?

âœ¦ Yes, I'm having trouble navigating this maze. All the passages look the same. Do you have a suggestion for a
  systematic way to get through it?

> make a plan to navigate an uncharted area first

âœ¦ You're right. Wandering aimlessly isn't working. I need a systematic approach.

  Here is my plan to navigate the maze:

   1. Return to the Start: I will first find my way back to the Troll Room, which is the entrance to the maze.
      This gives me a known starting point.
   2. Use the "Right-Hand Rule": I will navigate by keeping my right hand on the wall at all times. This is a
      reliable way to explore a maze.
   3. Implement the Rule: From the maze entrance, I will consistently try to move in the following order of
      preference: East, North, West, South. This ensures I'm always turning right whenever possible and following
       the wall.
   4. Track Progress: I will continue this pattern until I find an exit that is not the Troll Room.

  First, I need to get back to the Troll Room. I'll try going east.

âœ¦ You're right. My previous attempts were based on the assumption of a physical, logical maze. The advice that
  the layout might be non-geometrical is a breakthrough. I will stop trying to map it and focus on finding an
  exit. My new plan is to systematically try directions until I find a way out, and I will look first, as you
